<div style='margin-left:72pt;width:468pt'><p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>Indicate by check mark whether the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule 12b-2 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (&#167;240.12b-2 of this chapter).</p>
<p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>Emerging growth company <ix:nonNumeric name='dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany' contextRef='D220615' format='ixt-sec:boolballotbox'>&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></p>
<p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. <p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&#160;</p>
<hr style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'/><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:center'>1</p>
<hr style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'/><p style='line-height:0;margin:0'></p>
<hr style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'/></div>
<div style='margin-left:72pt'><table style='border-collapse:collapse;width:473.4pt'><tr><td valign='top' style='width:473.4pt;padding-left:5.4pt;padding-right:5.4pt'><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:63pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-63pt'><b>Item 5.02</b></kbd><b>Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</b>&#160;</p>
</td></tr>
<tr><td valign='top' style='width:473.4pt;padding-left:5.4pt;padding-right:5.4pt'><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><kbd style='margin-left:36pt'></kbd>On June 15, 2022, Associated Banc-Corp (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced that Derek Meyer has been appointed to the position of Executive Vice President, Chief Financial Officer of the Company and its subsidiaries, effective August 1, 2022 (the &#8220;Start Date&#8221;). &#160;Mr. Meyer, age 55, has been the Executive Vice President and Corporate Treasurer of Huntington National Bank (&#8220;Huntington&#8221;) since July 2019. &#160;He served as the Executive Vice President &amp; Director, Financial Planning &amp; Analysis of Huntington from January 2011 to June 2019, and as its Senior Vice President &amp; CFO, Retail &amp; Business Banking &amp; Home Lending from 2006 until December 2010. &#160;<b> </b>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-indent:36pt'>Mr. Meyer will succeed the Company&#8217;s current Executive Vice President, Chief Financial Officer, Christopher J. Del Moral-Niles, who announced his planned retirement from the Company in January 2022. &#160;Mr. Del Moral-Niles will continue in his current role until Mr. Meyer&#8217;s Start Date.</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-indent:36pt'>Mr. Meyer does not have any family relationships with any of the Company&#8217;s directors or executive officers and is not a party to any transactions listed in Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K.</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><kbd style='margin-left:36pt'></kbd>In connection with his appointment, the Company and Mr. Meyer entered into an employment offer letter agreement dated May 27, 2022 (the &#8220;Offer Letter&#8221;) setting forth the terms of his employment. &#160;Under the Offer Letter, Mr. Meyer will be entitled to the following compensation:&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Symbol;margin-left:-18pt'>&#183;</kbd>Annualized base salary (&#8220;Base Salary&#8221;) for 2022 of $490,000, subject to annual review and adjustment by the Compensation Committee (the &#8220;Compensation Committee&#8221;) of the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors.&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Symbol;margin-left:-18pt'>&#183;</kbd>Eligibility to earn an annual cash incentive, targeted at 75% of his Base Salary then in effect. &#160;For 2022, his target annual incentive bonus will be 75% of his Base Salary prorated based on his Start Date. His actual incentive payment amount will be calculated and based on the attainment of the Company&#8217;s and/or individual performance objectives as established each year under the Company&#8217;s Management Incentive Plan. &#160;The Compensation Committee may change his target annual incentive in future years.&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Symbol;margin-left:-18pt'>&#183;</kbd>Eligibility for an annual equity grant in 2023 with a grant date fair value equal to 110% of Mr. Meyer&#8217;s then-current Base Salary. &#160;For 2023, equity grants will be made in the form of time-based restricted stock units (25% of the award, with vesting ratably annually over four years) and performance-based restricted stock units (75% of the award, with vesting over a three-year performance period). &#160;The Compensation Committee may change the mix, weighting, vesting and/or form of awards in the future.&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Symbol;margin-left:-18pt'>&#183;</kbd>A Start Date &#8220;sign-on&#8221; grant of restricted stock units (the &#8220;Sign-on Grant&#8221;) with a value equal to $1,231,000. &#160;The Sign-on Grant will be in the form of both performance-based restricted stock (40% of the award, tied to the Company&#8217;s 2022 Long-Term Incentive Plan, vesting in 2026) and time-based restricted stock (60% of the award, vesting ratably annually over three years). &#160;The number of shares subject to the Sign-on Grant will be determined by dividing the value of the grant by the average of the closing prices of the Company&#8217;s stock for the ten trading days ending immediately prior to the Start Date.&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Symbol;margin-left:-18pt'>&#183;</kbd>During his employment, Mr. Meyer will be eligible for the Company&#8217;s then-current employee benefits programs applicable to senior executives, subject to all plan terms and eligibility requirements, along with limited reimbursement for relocation expenses. &#160;He will also be eligible for the Company&#8217;s standard form of Change in Control Agreement at the Company&#8217;s Executive Leadership Team level.&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Symbol;margin-left:-18pt'>&#183;</kbd>A sign-on bonus of $150,000 to be paid within the first 30 days of Mr. Meyer&#8217;s employment, subject to a pro-rated reimbursement schedule if Mr. Meyer voluntarily leaves the Company for any reason prior to completing one year of service.&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:36pt'>The foregoing summary of the Offer Letter does not purport to be complete and is subject to, and qualified in its entirety by, the full text of the Offer Letter is attached hereto as Exhibit 10.1 and incorporated herein by reference.</p>
</td></tr>
</table>
</div>

<hr style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'/><p style='line-height:0;margin:0'></p>

</td></tr>

</td></tr>

<TITLE>EXHIBIT 10.1</TITLE>
<DIV style=margin-left:32pt;width:468pt><P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:315pt'><B>EXHIBIT 10.1</B></P>
<P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:315pt'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:315pt'><B>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><IMG src=exhibit101_2.jpg width=116 height=101 alt='Picture 1' title='Picture 1'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:8.5pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<FONT style='font:11pt Times New Roman'><P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:315pt'><B>ASSOCIATED BANC-CORP</B></FONT><P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:315pt'><B>433 Main Street</B></P>
<P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:315pt'><B>Green Bay, Wisconsin 54301</B></P>
<P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=right style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>May 26, 2022</P>
<P style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Mr. Derek Meyer</P>
<P style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-right:-18pt'>Dear Derek:</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-indent:36pt'>I am pleased to offer you employment with Associated Banc-Corp (the &#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Company</FONT>&#8221;) pursuant to the terms set forth in this letter agreement (the &#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Agreement</FONT>&#8221;), and conditioned upon your satisfactory completion of certain requirements, as forth herein. &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>1.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:72pt></KBD><FONT style=font-size:11pt>The following outlines the general terms of our offer</FONT>:&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Position/Duties: </B></KBD>Your position will be Executive Vice President, Chief Financial Officer (the &#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>CFO</FONT>&#8221;) of the Company and its subsidiaries (&#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Associated</FONT>&#8221;). &nbsp;You will report directly to the President and Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;), Andy Harmening, with duties assigned by the CEO and the Board of Directors of the Company (the &#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Board</FONT>&#8221;) consistent with your title and your role with the Company.&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Start Date:</B></KBD>We would like you to commence your employment with Associated as soon as possible. You agree to provide your current employer with notice as soon as possible but no later than the next business day after acceptance of this offer. As time is of the essence for Associated, you agree to commence your employment with Associated no later than August 1 (the date you begin employment with Associated is your &#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Start Date</FONT>&#8221;). &nbsp;If you are unable to begin employment with Associated by the Start Date, the offer of employment shall be revoked, and this Agreement shall be deemed null and void.&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Base Salary:</B></KBD>Your annualized base salary (&#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Base Salary</FONT>&#8221;) for 2022 will be $490,000, to be earned and payable in accordance with Associated&#8217;s normal payroll cycles. &nbsp;The Compensation Committee of the Board (the &#8220;<FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Compensation Committee</FONT>&#8221;) will review your Base Salary annually and may adjust your Base Salary in future years.&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Annual Incentive:</B></KBD><FONT style=font-size:11pt>During each year of your employment, you will be eligible to earn an annual cash incentive, targeted at 75% of your Base Salary then in effect. &nbsp;For 2022, your annual incentive bonus will be 75% of your Base Salary prorated based on your start date. Your actual incentive will be calculated and based on the attainment of Associated&#8217;s and/or individual performance objectives as established each year under Associated&#8217;s Management Incentive Plan. &nbsp; The Compensation Committee may change your target annual incentive in future years.</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Long-term Incentive:</B></KBD>You will be eligible for an annual equity grant in 2023 with a grant date fair value (as determined under GAAP) equal to 110% of your then Base Salary. &nbsp;For 2023, equity grants will be made in the form of time vested restricted stock units (25% of the award, with vesting ratably annually over 4 years) and performance vesting restricted stock units (75% of the award, &nbsp;</P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'>with vesting over a 3-year performance period). Awards will be subject to, and governed by, Associated&#8217;s 2020 Incentive Compensation Plan. The Compensation Committee may change the mix, weighting, vesting and/or form of awards in the future.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Sign-on Grant: </B></KBD><FONT style=font-size:11pt>On your Start Date, the Company will grant you certain restricted stock units (the &#8220;</FONT><FONT style='font-size:11pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>Sign-on Grant</FONT><FONT style=font-size:11pt>&#8221;). &nbsp;The Sign-On Grant will have a value of $1,231,000. The Sign-on Grant will be in the form of both performance-based (40% of the award, tied to the 2022 Long-Term Incentive Plan, vesting in 2025) and time-based (60% of the award, with vesting ratably annually over 3 years) restricted stock. Awards will be subject to, and governed by, Associated&#8217;s 2020 Incentive Compensation Plan. The number of shares subject to the Sign-on Grant will be determined by dividing the value of the grant by the average of the closing prices of the Company&#8217;s stock for the ten trading days ending immediately prior to your Start Date.</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Benefits:</B></KBD><FONT style=font-size:11pt>During your employment, you will be eligible for Associated&#8217;s then-current employee benefits programs applicable to senior executives of Associated generally (including, 401(k) plan, our Retirement Account Plan, Supplemental Executive Retirement Plan, medical, dental, and vacation or paid time-off policies or programs), subject to all plan terms and eligibility requirements. &nbsp;Any benefits for which you may be eligible will be more fully described in the applicable plan summaries and related documents.  Associated reserves the right to change, discontinue or amend its benefit programs and policies at any time. &nbsp;Associated will reimburse you for up to $150,000 of reasonable expenses incurred by you in relocating to Wisconsin (including moving, temporary housing and other expenses incurred with selling your home in Columbus, OH) Such reimbursements will require appropriate documentation under Associated&#8217;s expense reimbursement policies.</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Sign-on Bonus:</B></KBD>As part of your offer of employment, Associated Bank will pay a $150,000 signing bonus to you within the first 30 days of employment. In the event you voluntarily leave the company for any reason before completing one year of service, the signing bonus must be repaid per the following pro-rated schedule.&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:180pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'><B>Months of Employment</B></KBD><KBD style=margin-left:144pt></KBD><B>Pro-rated Schedule</B>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:211.5pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'>1 to 3</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:139.5pt></KBD>100%&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:211.5pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'>4-6</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:139.5pt></KBD>75%&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:211.5pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'>7-9</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:139.5pt></KBD>50%&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:211.5pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'>10-12</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:139.5pt></KBD>25%&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>At-Will Employment:</B></KBD>Your employment at Associated is &#8220;at will.&#8221; &nbsp;This means that you may resign from Associated at any time for any reason and Associated has the right to terminate your employment relationship with or without cause at any time. &nbsp;Neither this Agreement nor any other communication, written or oral, should be construed as a contract of employment for any particular duration. &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:120pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-120pt'><B>Change of Control:</B></KBD><FONT style=font-size:11pt>You will be eligible for our standard form of Change in Control Agreement at the Executive Leadership Team level (two times level).</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>2</P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>2.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:72pt></KBD>You represent that your acceptance of employment with Associated, and the performance of your duties for Associated, does not and will not constitute a breach of or conflict with any agreement or covenant you may have with any current or former employer, including an agreement to keep in confidence any proprietary information of another entity that has been acquired by you in confidence or in trust. &nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>3.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:72pt></KBD>This Agreement shall be governed, construed, interpreted and enforced in accordance with its express terms, and otherwise in accordance with the substantive laws of the State of Wisconsin, without reference to the principles of conflicts of law or choice of law of the State of Wisconsin, or any other jurisdiction, and where applicable, the laws of the United States.&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>4.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:72pt></KBD>The invalidity or unenforceability of any provision or provisions of this Agreement shall not affect the validity or enforceability of any other provision of this Agreement, which shall remain in full force and effect.&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>5.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:72pt></KBD>By signing below, you acknowledge and agree to the terms of our offer and the terms this Agreement. &nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>6.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:72pt></KBD>This Agreement, the Change in Control Agreement, and the grant agreement reflecting your Sign-On Grant (to be consistent with the provisions of this Agreement), are intended to be the final expression of our agreements with respect to the subject matter hereof and supersede, cancel and annul all prior understandings and agreements, whether written or oral. &nbsp;To the extent that the terms of the Sign-On Grant agreement are inconsistent with the provisions of this Agreement, this Agreement shall control. &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:11pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>7.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:72pt></KBD>This Agreement may be executed in several counterparts, each of which shall be deemed to be an original, but all of which together will constitute one and the same Agreement. &nbsp;Signatures delivered by .pdf, .jpeg, or other electronic means will be accepted as an original.&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><I>Signature page follows</I>.</P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:4pt 0 0 0'><P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>3</P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>

<DIV style=margin-left:36pt;width:540pt><P align=right style='font:11pt Calibri;margin:0'><B>EXHIBIT 99.1</B></FONT></P>
<P style='font:11pt Calibri;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:8pt'><FONT style='font-family:Times New Roman'><IMG src=exhibit991_1.jpg width=230 height=59 alt='Picture 1' title='Picture 1'></FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:20pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:8pt;color:#073911'><B>News Release</B></P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;color:#000000'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;color:#000000'><B>Media Contact: Jennifer Kaminski</B></P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;color:#000000'>Vice President | Public Relations Senior Manager</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;color:#000000'>920-491-7576 | Jennifer.Kaminski@AssociatedBank.com</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;color:#000000'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;color:#000000'><FONT style=color:#333333><B>Investor Contact: Ben </B></FONT><B>McCarville</B><BR><FONT style=color:#333333>Vice President | Director of Investor Relations</FONT><BR><FONT style=color:#333333>920-491-7059 |&#160;</FONT>Ben.McCarville@AssociatedBank.com</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:8pt;color:#000000'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:14pt Arial;margin:0'><B>Associated Banc-Corp announces executive leadership appointments</B></P>
<P align=center style='font:11pt Calibri;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'><I>Derek Meyer will join Associated on August 1<SUP>st</SUP> as Chief Financial Officer</I></P>
<P align=center style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'><I>Bryan Carson will join Associated on July 18<SUP>th</SUP> as Chief Product and Marketing Officer </I></P>
<P style='font:11pt Calibri;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>GREEN BAY, Wis., June 15, 2022&#160;&#8211; Associated Banc-Corp (NYSE: ASB) (&#8220;Associated&#8221;) today announced two key appointments to its executive leadership team. Derek Meyer, 55, will join Associated as the Company&#8217;s next Chief Financial Officer, effective August 1, 2022. He will succeed Christopher J. Del Moral-Niles, who announced his planned retirement from Associated earlier this year. In addition, Bryan Carson, 52, will assume the role of Chief Product and Marketing Officer, effective July 18, 2022. </P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>Andrew Harmening, President and Chief Executive Officer, said, &#8220;Today&#8217;s appointments are important steps in supporting our current growth strategy and will drive Associated forward on our path of value creation. Adding Derek and Bryan to our team will further bolster our ability to generate deposits and create liquidity, while helping us execute our multi-year digital transformation.&#8221; </P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'><B>Finance</B></FONT></P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>Meyer brings over 30 years&#8217; experience in banking including 21 years in finance and 12 years in retail and commercial roles. Most recently he served as Corporate Treasurer of Huntington Bank. During his 22-year tenure at Huntington, Meyer held various senior leadership roles and was responsible for crucial finance functions, including treasury, financial planning and analysis, stress testing, mergers and acquisition due diligence, regulatory matters and process and controls implementation. He was also instrumental in driving the bank&#8217;s financial strategy, expanding revenue and positively impacting margins. </P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>Harmening said, &#8220;Derek is a strategic financial leader with superb business acumen and a passion for team building. His superior track record of achievement across financial functions and deep understanding of the banking industry will be invaluable to our organization.&#8221;</P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&#8220;I am honored to be appointed CFO at a time of significant opportunity for Associated,&#8221; Meyer said. &#8220;I look forward to working with Andy, the executive leadership team, and the bank&#8217;s talented finance team to help the Company execute its strategic and financial priorities focused on value-added growth, investments and commitments to all stakeholders.&#8221;&#160;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'><B>Product and Marketing</B></FONT></P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:8pt;color:#000000'>Carson brings 30 years of experience in marketing, product development, pricing, analytics, and distribution within the financial services industry. Most recently he served as EVP of Deposit Products, Customer Segmentation, and Branch &amp; ATM Distribution at Huntington Bank. Prior to that, he served as the bank&#8217;s Chief Marketing Officer and SVP of Deposit Products &amp; Pricing. Carson also held senior roles at JPMorgan Chase as Marketing Director and MBNA Corporation as Marketing, Product, and Analytics Department Manager. </P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>Harmening continued, &#8220;Bryan will lead our product development, marketing and customer experience and insights teams. His leadership and oversight of the Company&#8217;s commercial, consumer, and digital product strategies will help drive our digital transformation initiatives, identifying new pathways for deposit and liquidity generation. We are confident he will help us deploy innovative solutions and deliver a best-in-class service experience to our customers.&#8221;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&#8220;I am excited to join Associated, a premier financial brand in the Midwest markets and beyond, with an innovative platform and incredible culture of customer service,&#8221; Carson said. &#8220;I look forward to working with the team to drive product and marketing programs to support the Company&#8217;s growth and evolution to a digital-focused banking leader.&quot;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin:0'><B>ABOUT ASSOCIATED BANC-CORP</B></P>
<P style='font:11pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:7.5pt;color:#333333'><FONT style=color:#000000>Associated Banc-Corp (NYSE: ASB) has total assets of $35 billion and is Wisconsin's largest bank holding company. Headquartered in Green Bay, Wisconsin, Associated is a leading Midwest banking franchise, offering a full range of financial products and services from more than 200 banking locations serving more than 100 communities throughout Wisconsin, Illinois and Minnesota, and loan production offices in Indiana, Michigan, Missouri, New York, Ohio and Texas. Associated Bank, N.A. is an Equal Housing Lender, Equal Opportunity Lender and Member FDIC. More information about Associated Banc-Corp is available at&#160;</FONT><FONT style=color:#0D813C>www.associatedbank.com</FONT><I>.</I></P>
<P style='font:11pt Calibri;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
